import pandas as pd
from sklearn.neural_network import MLPClassifier
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, classification_report

Para facilitar o entendimento do banco de dados, exclui-se a coluna 13 que no necessria e renomeia-se as colunas.

In [2]:
data = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data = data.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

EXPERIMENTO 1

Utiliza-se apenas 20% dos dados do banco de dados para usar como treinamento e o restante ser alocado para uso no teste.

In [4]:
x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=15)

Utiliza-se trs camadas de unidades de processamento intermedirio, a funo sigmoidal como funo de ativao e 500 como nmrero mximo de interaes.

Como pode-se ver, chegou-se a uma acurcia de 82% utilizando essa configurao de MLP.

In [7]:
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

              precision    recall  f1-score   support

    Abnormal       0.88      0.86      0.87        44
      Normal       0.68      0.72      0.70        18

    accuracy                           0.82        62
   macro avg       0.78      0.79      0.79        62
weighted avg       0.83      0.82      0.82        62

O relatrio nos mostra que obteve-se uma precision de 88% nos casos anormais e 68% nos casos normais, e um recall de 86% nos casos anormais e 72% nos casos normais.

A sinalizao de warning diz que o nmero limite de interaes foi alcanado, porm a otmizao ainda no convergiu. Iremos dobrar o nmero de interaes e verificaremos como o MPL se comporta com os mesmos valores de hidden_layer_sizes e aps com os valores dobrados hidden_layer_sizes.

EXPERIMENTO 2

O caso em que apenas duplicamos o nmero de interaes

In [14]:
y.value_counts()
Out[14]:
Abnormal    210
Normal      100
Name: class, dtype: int64

Como o banco de dados desbalanceado, visto o nmero de casos anormais e normais, o valor da acurcia no um boa mtrica para avaliar a MLP, portanto, deve-se atentar as mtricas precision e recall do report, pois so elas que nos diro se o MLP est classificando corretamente os casos. Precision se diz respeito a porcentagem dos casos selecionados daquela classe que foram classificados corretamente, j recall significa a porcentagem dos casos totais daquela classe que seriam classificados corretamente.

Vamos agora alterar alguns dos parmetros da MLP:

EXPERIMENTO 4

In [15]:
x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size=0.3, random_state=15)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,100,100), activation='logistic', max_iter=500, random_state=42, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

Vamos agora tentar descobrir quais so as melhores variveis para utilizar no nosso banco de dados da MLP para tentar maximizar a preciso dos casos.

In [16]:
from sklearn.ensemble import ExtraTreesClassifier
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
model = ExtraTreesClassifier()
model.fit(x,y)
feat_importances = pd.Series(model.feature_importances_, index=x.columns)
feat_importances.nlargest(12).plot(kind='barh')
plt.show()

O grfico nos mostra em ordem cresente as variveis que mais impactam na classificao dos casos, logo, vamos descartar as primeiras 6 e utilizar o resto.

In [17]:
new_data = data[['degree_spondylolisthesis', 'pelvic_radius', 'pelvic_incidence', 'pelvic_tilt', 'lumbar_lordosis_angle', 'sacral_slope', 'class']]
y = new_data['class']
x = new_data.drop(['class'], axis = 1)

EXPERIMENTO 5

Vamos treinar vrias configuraes de MLP para tentar descobrir uma possvel boa implementao de MLP para o problema.

In [18]:
x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=15)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,50,25,), activation='logistic', max_iter=500, random_state=42, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

Pode-se ver que as ltimas duas configuraes de MLP apresentam excelentes resultados de acurcia, precision e recall, portanto, so possveis boas candidatas a serem implementadas.

A equipe levantou a hiptese de que o fato de a quantidade de dados "Abnormal" estar acima da quantidade de dados "Normal" est baixando a preciso para classificao de dados "Normal" nos primeiros exemplos deste ralatrio e baixando a acurcia geral nos dois exemplos acima (melhores resultados at ento). Para testar isso, vamos igualar a quantidade de dados "Abnormal" e "Normal" com duas abordagens. Primeiro, expluindo os 110 primeiros dados "Abnormal" e depois, excluindo 110 dados "Abnormal" de modo aleatrio.

EXPERIMENTO 9

Abaixo, segue o exemplo excluindo os 110 primeiros dados "Abnormal", utilizando o dataset do primeiro experimento e o MLP classifier do primeiro experimento, ou seja, antes da aplicao de todas as melhorias propostas pelos experimentos acima:

In [22]:
data1 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data1 = data1.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data1.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

new_data_copy = data1

new_data3 = new_data_copy.copy()

for i in range(110):
    new_data3.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data3['class']
x = new_data3.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.2, random_state=15)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,50,25,), activation='logistic', max_iter=500, random_state=42, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

Abnormal    100

Iteration 2, loss = 0.70216837

data2 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data2 = data2.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data2.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

new_data_copy = data2

new_data4 = new_data_copy.copy()
new_data5 = new_data_copy.copy()
new_data6 = new_data_copy.copy()

for i in range(210):
    new_data5.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

for i in range(298):
    new_data6.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)
    
new_data4 = new_data4.append(new_data5, ignore_index=True)
new_data4 = new_data4.append(new_data6, ignore_index=True)

for i in range(2):
    new_data4.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data4['class']
x = new_data4.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.2, random_state=15)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,50,25,), activation='logistic', max_iter=500, random_state=42, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

data2 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data2 = data2.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data2.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

new_data_copy = data2

new_data4 = new_data_copy.copy()
new_data5 = new_data_copy.copy()
new_data6 = new_data_copy.copy()

for i in range(210):
    new_data5.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

for i in range(298):
    new_data6.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)
    
new_data4 = new_data4.append(new_data5, ignore_index=True)
new_data4 = new_data4.append(new_data6, ignore_index=True)

for i in range(2):
    new_data4.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data4['class']
x = new_data4.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.1, random_state=13)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,300,500), max_iter=500, alpha=0.0001, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

EXPERIMENTO 12

Abaixo, segue o exemplo excluindo 110 dados "Abnormal" de forma randmica, utilizando o dataset do primeiro experimento e o MLP classifier do primeiro experimento, ou seja, antes da aplicao de todas as melhorias propostas pelos experimentos acima. A inteno, assim como no experimento passado, igualar o nmero de casos "Abnormal" e "Normal", mas agora de modo randmico:

In [25]:
import random
data1 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data1 = data1.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data1.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

new_data_copy = data1

new_data3 = new_data_copy.copy()

range_list = random.sample(range(210), 110)

for i in range_list:
    new_data3.drop(i,axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data3['class']
x = new_data3.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.2, random_state=15)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,50,25,), activation='logistic', max_iter=500, random_state=42, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred)
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

Normal      100

EXPERIMENTO 13

Agora, uniremos a melhor abordagem para igualar a quantidade de casos que retirar os 110 primeiros casos "Abnormal" do dataset com o melhor resultado das melhorias sugeridas na manipulao de parmetros do MLP:

In [26]:
data1 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data1 = data1.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data1.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence", 
    "Col2" : "pelvic_tilt",
    "Col3" : "lumbar_lordosis_angle",
    "Col4" : "sacral_slope", 
    "Col5" : "pelvic_radius",
    "Col6" : "degree_spondylolisthesis", 
    "Col7" : "pelvic_slope",
    "Col8" : "direct_tilt",
    "Col9" : "thoracic_slope", 
    "Col10" :"cervical_tilt", 
    "Col11" : "sacrum_angle",
    "Col12" : "scoliosis_slope", 
    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

new_data_copy = data1

new_data3 = new_data_copy.copy()

for i in range(110):
    new_data3.drop((i+1),axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data3['class']
x = new_data3.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.1, random_state=13)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,300,500), max_iter=500, alpha=0.0001, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

EXPERIMENTO 14

Agora tentaremos uma abordagem similar do experimento anterior, unindo as melhorias nos parmetros MLP com o ato de igualar o nmero de casos, mas agora de modo randmico:

In [27]:
data1 = pd.read_csv("Dataset_spine.csv")
data1 = data1.drop(['Unnamed: 13'], axis=1)
data1.rename(columns = {
    "Col1" : "pelvic_incidence",

    "Class_att" : "class"}, inplace=True)

for i in range_list:
    new_data3.drop(i,axis=0,inplace=True)

y = new_data3['class']
x = new_data3.drop(['class'], axis = 1)
print(y.value_counts())

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size= 0.1, random_state=13)
clf = MLPClassifier(hidden_layer_sizes=(100,300,500), max_iter=500, alpha=0.0001, verbose=True)
clf.fit(x_train, y_train)
y_pred = clf.predict(x_test)
print(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)

In [36]:

In [37]:

report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred)
print(report)
